@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

#################
#Special Titles
#################

e_tamriel = {
	color = { 150 0 0 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	
	capital = c_imperial_city

	ai_primary_priority = {
		add = @always_primary_score
	}
}

e_ghost_sea = {
	color = { 100 0 0 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	
	capital = c_volkihar
}

e_reach = {
	color = { 15 110 15 }
	color2 = { 255 255 255 }
	
	capital = c_markarth

	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = { culture = culture:reachfolk }
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
}
